01.1 Tkinter Hello World Lab¶

This is the basic building blocks for the Python Tkinter window.

  • Contents:

    1. Google Slides Link

    2. Repl.it Link

    3. Lab Overview - What is required.

      a. GUI Solution - This is what the final outcome should look like.

      b. READ.ME File - This is the objectives and rubric.

      c. Build.ME file- This is the code needed to complete the lab.

This lab and Google Slides covers the following content:

  • Syntax for defining a window
  • Tkinter Library import
  • Tk() class instance
  • .geometry method
  • .title method
  • .mainloop method

  • Change title to read "Hello World"
  • Modify window size: height=500 and width=450

c. The 'Build.ME' File¶

This file includes all the code necessary to get the lab up and running. It is divided into important sections.¶

In [ ]:
#  Resources:
#    https://www.studytonight.com/tkinter/python-tkinter-canvas-widget
#
#  This lab creates the basic python tkinter window.  
#   This "window" is an empty container waiting for widgets.
#    It does nothing!

#   Steps required to run:

#     1. import * (ALL) the tkinter libraries
from tkinter import *   

#     2. The Tk() class instance is assigned to the variable named top
top = Tk()  

#     3. The .geometry method is used to set height and width of window  
top.geometry("100x100")  

#     4. The .title method is used to set height and width of window  
top.title("Change to say hi to the people of the world...") 

#     5. The .mainloop method is used to keep the window active/visible.  
top.mainloop()

#   Objectives:
#       Change title to read "hello world"
#       Modify window size to be a height=500 and width=450


Top
